[03:08:45] introduction the magic of of the Book of
[03:08:48] the Dead of the Egyptian Book of the
[03:08:50] Dead by EA Wallace budge this LibriVox
[03:08:54] recording is in the public
[03:08:56] domain introduction the magic of the
[03:08:59] Book of the Dead the Egyptians from the
[03:09:02] earliest to the latest period of their
[03:09:05] history were addicted to the use of
[03:09:07] formula which were thought to be able to
[03:09:09] affect results usually beyond the power
[03:09:12] of man and they accompanied such formula
[03:09:15] with the performance of certain
[03:09:16] ceremonies
[03:09:18] the formula consisted of the repetition
[03:09:20] of the names of gods and supernatural
[03:09:23] beings benevolent or hostile to man as
[03:09:26] the case might be and of in treaties or
[03:09:29] curses the ceremonies were of various
[03:09:32] kinds and the object of the present
[03:09:34] chapter is to describe briefly those
[03:09:36] which relate to the various sections of
[03:09:38] the Book of the Dead the Egyptian
[03:09:41] believe that every word spoken under
[03:09:43] certain circumstances must be followed
[03:09:46] by some effect good or bad a Prayer
[03:09:49] uttered by a properly qualified person
[03:09:52] or by a man ceremonially pure in the
[03:09:55] proper place and in the proper manner
[03:09:57] must necessarily be answered
[03:10:00] favorably and similarly the curses which
[03:10:03] were pronounced Upon A man or beast or
[03:10:05] thing in the name of a hostile
[03:10:07] supernatural being were bound to result
[03:10:10] in harm to the object cursed it seems
[03:10:13] that this idea had its origin in the
[03:10:15] belief that the world and all that
[03:10:18] therein is came into being immediately
[03:10:21] after th had interpreted in words the
[03:10:25] will of the deity in respect of the
[03:10:27] creation of the world and that creation
[03:10:30] was the result of the God's command in
[03:10:33] very early times the Egyptian called in
[03:10:36] the professional religious man to utter
[03:10:38] words of good omen over the dead body of
[03:10:41] his relative or friend and later the
[03:10:44] same words written upon some substance
[03:10:46] and buried with him were believed to be
[03:10:49] effectual in procuring for him the good
[03:10:51] things of the life beyond the grave in
[03:10:54] the text on the Pyramid of unas is a
[03:10:58] reference to something written which the
[03:11:00] deceased was supposed to possess in the
[03:11:02] following words the bone and flesh which
[03:11:05] have no writing are wretched but behold
[03:11:08] the writing of unas is under the Great
[03:11:11] Seal and behold it is not under the
[03:11:14] little seal and in the text Stone the
[03:11:17] Pyramid of Pepe the first we find the
[03:11:19] words the Urus of this Pepe is upon his
[03:11:23] head there is a writing on each side of
[03:11:26] him and he hath words of magical power
[03:11:28] at his two feet thus equipped the King
[03:11:32] enters heaven in the reign of chops
[03:11:36] however we are told that his second son
